  # Summer 2026 Tech Internships by Pitt CSC & Simplify

  We're back! Use this repo to share and keep track of **Summer 2026 tech internships** across software, data science, quant, and more. The list is updated and maintained daily by the [Pitt Computer Science Club](https://pittcsc.org/) and [Simplify](https://simplify.jobs/)!


  üß† For valuable tips on navigating the internship process, be sure to check out our guide: [**Zero to Offer**](https://web.archive.org/web/20250319235510/https://pittcs.wiki/zero-to-offer/) üß† 

  üôè **Contribute by submitting an [issue](https://github.com/SimplifyJobs/Summer2026-Internships/issues/new/choose)! See the contribution guidelines [here](./CONTRIBUTING.md)!** üôè

  ## Legend

  üõÇ Does NOT offer sponsorship

  üá∫üá∏ Requires U.S. Citizenship

  üîí Internship application is closed

  üî• FAANG+ company

  üéì Advanced degree required (Master's, PhD, MBA)
